About This Space

Sometimes the thing you're looking for finds you first.

That's what writing became for me.

And if you're here, maybe something is finding you too.

I write about what I see, what stays, and the people I meet along the way.

Scrolls

From the In-Between

What I witness. What I write. What I carry. What becomes prayer.

Reflection

The prayer I kept saying even when I stopped believing it

On intercession, muscle memory, and what faith looks like when it runs on empty.

Faith

What the valley actually looks like from inside it

Not a metaphor. A testimony about the night my son went missing and what I learned about God in the silence.

Becoming

She baked because she knew something we didn't

On my great-aunt's kitchen, the things she never said out loud, and the recipes that outlasted her.

Voice

Your confession goes ahead of you

The words Pastor Neva said that stopped me mid-step — and the forty days of prayer that followed.
